  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_62732f18-eb43-482b-9dac-43c3f0060392'
      });
    }

<div id="review_794473512" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/794473512" />
    <a title="K" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16359109-k"><img alt="K" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1357989852p2/16359109.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/794473512?book_show_action=true">Dec 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K" href="/user/show/16359109-k">K</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=sweet-hero">sweet-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=heart-wrenching">heart-wrenching</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=college">college</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=exhausting-read">exhausting-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer794473512" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10864917575053488827"><b>4 Not Much Left of Me Stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387873844i/7687377.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>'Someone once told me that it’s not about whether there is life after you die, but whether you’re alive before you die. I didn't believe I could ever feel alive again. Not until Parker.' I am Aundrea McCall, and I am a survivor.'</b><br/><blockquote>
  <i>Cancer.<br/>It can break you.<br/>Or it can make you stronger. <br/>I choose stronger.<br/>I choose survival.</i>
</blockquote><br/><b>Wow, this one's a tearjerker!</b><br/><br/><i>What's Left of Me</i> had me hooked from the first page! I rarely put it down, only when necessary, for I had to find out wha</span>
  <span id="freeText10864917575053488827" style="display:none"><b>4 Not Much Left of Me Stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387873844i/7687377.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>'Someone once told me that it’s not about whether there is life after you die, but whether you’re alive before you die. I didn't believe I could ever feel alive again. Not until Parker.' I am Aundrea McCall, and I am a survivor.'</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>Cancer.<br>It can break you.<br>Or it can make you stronger. <br>I choose stronger.<br>I choose survival.</i>
</blockquote><br><b>Wow, this one's a tearjerker!</b><br><br><i>What's Left of Me</i> had me hooked from the first page! I rarely put it down, only when necessary, for I had to find out what would happen to Aundrea and Parker next! Would she live or die? HEA or NSHEA? Let me start off by saying that when I read the blurb for this book I knew it would be a sad book. What book about cancer isn't? Still, I thought I was prepared. I thought I could handle it without crying..and I was wrong yet again. I cried ugly tears while reading this book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Aundrea, you have already left your mark.” Picking up my hand, he places it over his heart. "Right here. You, Aundrea Leigh McCall, are the beat of my heart. I will give you my own breath, if it means keeping you alive."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387950161i/7704989.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br><i>What's Left of Me</i> is about Aundrea and Parker. Aundrea was an amazing heroine to read about. She's tough yet vulnerable. You see, Aundrea has cancer. Has had cancer for 4 years now. She's the type of heroine that hates people taking care of her, hate's feeling helpless + lifeless. Everything changes when she meets Parker though. Parker, the young new veterinarian who works with her brother in law. Parker makes Andrea feel truly beautiful for the first time in her life. He shows her what it is to live. He teaches her that even though she's been dealt a shitty lot in life, she can still come out on top.<br><br>The only problem however is that Parker doesn't know that Aundrea has cancer. And Aundrea has no intentions of telling him... <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"How do you tell someone you love that you have cancer? That you're slowly slipping away? That your body is floating away from you? There is no right time. No right moment. No right words. Words I need to speak. Words I need to form, but can't seem to get out."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387952041i/7705387.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is mostly about the journey of Aundrea and Parker together as they fall in love. The whole time you're reading it's heartbreaking, because you know that eventually the balls going to drop and Parker is either going to find out she has cancer or she's going to have to tell him herself. So sad, the lengths she goes through to hide it from him. My heart broke for both of them. Their love for each other was so strong and true. I never doubted it for a minute. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You own me, Aundrea. I couldn’t walk away from you if I tried. The second I laid eyes on you that night, in the mirror, I knew it.” He takes my hands in his, squeezing gently. “I would be a damn fool to let you slip away from me. I am so unbelievably in love with you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I'm not going to say much more on that topic for I don't want to spoil this book for anyone. Just be prepared to bring tissues. I was absolutely amazed that this is Amanda Maxlyn's first book, for if the writing is profound enough to make me cry, then that's the mark of a great book! Well done! The only thing that prevents me from giving this book 5 stars is the ending. I HATED it. I'm sure some people won't be bothered by it, but I didn't like it. AT ALL. While I really really liked this one, I just wish the ending left me with a little something more. However don't let that deter you for this is still a fantastic read and I highly recommend it! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I’m scared that I’m going to go through life without leaving a trace of myself behind. I want to do things like travel, or be spontaneous, to show that even after I’m gone, I’ve left a small trace of me behind. I’m afraid that one morning I simply won’t wake up and there won’t be anything to show for the life I’ve lived."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387947040i/7703304.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"More tears fall. I never thought of myself as one of those women. The type who get all sappy when a man says they love them, or vice versa, but now I understand why they do, because it’s in this<br>moment that I know I’ve found the person I was meant to be with."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10864917575053488827" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_752311964" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/752311964" />
    <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review"><img alt="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454474452p2/9816167.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/752311964?book_show_action=true">Oct 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review">Jessica&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer752311964" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12118860168591444186">What’s Left Of Me had me at EVERY page! I couldn’t put down my Kindle to eat, to clean, to sleep until I read to the end. It is such an emotional, yet sexy, fun, and sad read all in one. Because of books like What’s Left of Me is why I LOVE to read and why I LOVE book boyfriends because I have a new one and his name is Parker Jackson… he’s all mine ladies! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385008427i/7043926.jpg' width='275' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385008427i/7043927.jpg' width='275' height='290' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was immediately drawn into the story from the first page. What’s Left of Me is written in the point of view of 21 year-old Aundrea. At firs</span>
  <span id="freeText12118860168591444186" style="display:none">What’s Left Of Me had me at EVERY page! I couldn’t put down my Kindle to eat, to clean, to sleep until I read to the end. It is such an emotional, yet sexy, fun, and sad read all in one. Because of books like What’s Left of Me is why I LOVE to read and why I LOVE book boyfriends because I have a new one and his name is Parker Jackson… he’s all mine ladies! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385008427i/7043926.jpg" width="275" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385008427i/7043927.jpg" width="275" height="290" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was immediately drawn into the story from the first page. What’s Left of Me is written in the point of view of 21 year-old Aundrea. At first she seems like your typical college girl going out for the night with a group of girls but Aundrea is hiding has cancer and has been battling the fight against her sickness for four years. Aundrea is determined to have fun, let loose and enjoy herself while she is a new city where no one knows her as the girl with cancer. That is when she meets him…. She meets Parker and boy is it fun and sexy! They have a wild hot night together with Aundrea leaving early that morning hoping to never see him again… but of course she does.<br><br>Parker turns out to be her new brother in-law’s partner… did I mention he is HOT <i>older</i> veterinarian? Parker is persistent in getting Aundrea to go out with him but Aundrea doesn’t date… she doesn’t know what her life she has left and does not need to involve anyone else in her pain. They have this cute flirtatious friendship that is forming. Even though they already had sex they are still building up to something and I love that I was still eager for them to truly to get together. Parker is the sweetest, sexiest, most caring man ever in a book. I loved him but I also loved Aundrea. <br><br>The writing really got to me; it touched my soul just because of the amazing details the author had while explain everything Aundrea is/was going through to help her beat cancer. I have never had to go through with anyone close to me having to endure cancer or chemotherapy before and reading the words of what Aundrea was experiencing was heart wrenching; the moments she was losing her hair, in pain, the procedures. It was just awful to have to read about but what an amazing job the author did in really connecting her reader to Aundrea’s character, I wanted to be there for Aundrea holding her hand the entire time.<br><br>The book really deals going back and forth between Aundrea being afraid to let Parker close because she doesn’t know what life will bring her or take away and having to deal with having cancer and what it does to one’s body and soul. She hides everything from Parker and I was just waiting for the moment in the book when he would have to know what she was going through. There was just no way she could hide it any longer. I was on the edge of my seat waiting and waiting and wanting to know how Parker would react. <br><br>I love Aundrea and Parker’s relationship. They did not meet the conventional way and “hooked-up” immediately but they still had this great build-up since Aundrea wouldn’t let Parker get close to her. The ending had me in total shock face. I don’t even want to ruin it for you so I won’t say too much but just know WHATEVER you are thinking, you’re wrong and I will leave it at that!<br><br>What’s Left Of Me took me on a wonderful, sad yet sweet journey about living life to the fullest and loving the ones who are lucky enough to be part of your life. I am so happy I was able to experience it and meet Parker Jackson because he is my new book boyfriend… Oh yes he is! <br><br>I give What’s Left Of Me 4.5 Stars!<br><br><br><i>Book provided by the author in return for an honest review.</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382766162i/6182035.png" width="190" height="119" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Stay connected with my reviews, book news and more:<br><a href="http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog- Jessica’s Book Review</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/jessbookreview" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> </b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12118860168591444186" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_755738776" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/755738776" />
    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/755738776?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=heart-breaking-gut-wrenching">heart-breaking-gut-wrenching</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=love">love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=scorching-hot">scorching-hot</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755738776" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8674896029595485251">4.5--<b>Cancer Sucks and Parker Kicks Ass</b>--Stars!!<br/><br/>Despite the heavy undertones of the book, the blurb grabbed me. I knew this was going to be sad. I knew it was going to hurt my heart. But I was also hoping that it would make me smile too. And it did...and it make me sigh and it made me laugh. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>"My life changed the night I met Parker. He has shown me that it is possible to carry on with the life I was meant to live, showing the world that even though I was dealt a shitty hand in life, I still too</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText8674896029595485251" style="display:none">4.5--<b>Cancer Sucks and Parker Kicks Ass</b>--Stars!!<br /><br />Despite the heavy undertones of the book, the blurb grabbed me. I knew this was going to be sad. I knew it was going to hurt my heart. But I was also hoping that it would make me smile too. And it did...and it make me sigh and it made me laugh. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"My life changed the night I met Parker. He has shown me that it is possible to carry on with the life I was meant to live, showing the world that even though I was dealt a shitty hand in life, I still took the gamble and came out on top. <br /><br />I am Aundrea McCall, and I am a survivor."</i>
</b><br /><br />Aundrea was diagnosed with cancer at the age of 17....she's a fighter. She beat it once, only for it to come back again. Forced to leave her friends and family behind she moves in with her sister Genna to participate in a trial study. The doctors think it's her best chance at survival.<br /><br />One of her first nights there she meets Parker. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"A man I'm spending time with.<br />A man I enjoy spending time with.<br />A man who makes me laugh.<br />A man who makes me feel alive.<br />A man who makes me forget about the shit I have going on."</i>
</b><br /><br />Aundrea isn't looking for love or a relationship. Aundrea is scared. Scared of love. Scared of opening up. Scared of living. Scared of the unknown.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"You're scared, but just because you can't see your future, doesn't mean that I can't. I see it clearly because I can see mine."</i>
</b><br /><br />Aundrea and Parker start out as friends. But Parker wants Aundrea and he'll do whatever it takes to get her. <br /> <br /><b>
  <i>"I want all of you, Aundrea. Everything and anything that you will give me. I want it all. I want to be your legs when you can't walk. I want to be your arms when you're too weak to eat. I want to be there for you day and night."</i>
</b><br /><br />For once in her life, Aundrea doesn't want to be looked at as different. She's wants to be treated just like everyone else. She gets that with Parker. Because Parker doesn't know. He doesn't know that she's sick. He doesn't know that she has cancer. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I never thought I could love anyone as much as I love you Parker. I think back over the time we've shared, and....even though our time together hasn't been that long, it's been the best time of my life. I just want to go on living my life with you, leaving my mark."</i>
</b><br /><br />So many times I wanted to yell at Aundrea to just TELL PARKER THE TRUTH. Parker was PERFECTION. I fell in love with Parker. Everyones deserves their own Parker. He was kind, caring, gentle, loving. Every day that went by that he didn't know, broke my heart. I was scared for when he found out....I was scared for how he was going to find out...I was scared for how he would react. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Aundrea, I will marry you. I will have children with you. I will have a long life with you. You and I will take on this world together. It's you and me. I will have it no other way. I love you more than I have ever loved anyone, which is why I will fight for you until my dying breath."</i>
</b><br /><br />This was Aundrea's journey. Her battle against cancer. Her falling in love for the first time. Her learning to let go and live every day as if it might be her last. Her letting people in to be her strength in times of weakness. <br /><br />One woman. One battle. One love. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I am Aundrea McCall, and I am a survivor."</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8674896029595485251" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1268369902" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1268369902" />
    <a title="Jeannine Allison" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30604562-jeannine-allison"><img alt="Jeannine Allison" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1488001283p2/30604562.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1268369902?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jeannine Allison" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jeannine Allison" href="/user/show/30604562-jeannine-allison">Jeannine Allison</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23598458-what-s-left-of-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=bawling-like-a-baby">bawling-like-a-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=will-read-again">will-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=swoon">swoon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=love-the-heroine">love-the-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30604562-jeannine-allison?shelf=sweet-guys">sweet-guys</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1268369902" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17812968846789860637"><b>
  <i>4.5 Stars (Re-Read 7/28/2017)<br/><br/>5 Stars (First Read 6/1/2015)</i>
</b><br/><br/>**FREE on Amazon**<br/><br/>HOLY. SHIT. I have so much to say, and yet I'm speechless at the same time. I have a mild headache and red, puffy cheeks from crying so hard. This book made me feel so much... the good and the bad. I absolutely loved it, even minor annoyances seemed inconsequential to how much I enjoyed this. I'll address those first, so I can gush about this novel for the rest of my review:<br/><br/>1) There were a few editing errors, or real</span>
  <span id="freeText17812968846789860637" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>4.5 Stars (Re-Read 7/28/2017)<br><br>5 Stars (First Read 6/1/2015)</i>
</b><br><br>**FREE on Amazon**<br><br>HOLY. SHIT. I have so much to say, and yet I'm speechless at the same time. I have a mild headache and red, puffy cheeks from crying so hard. This book made me feel so much... the good and the bad. I absolutely loved it, even minor annoyances seemed inconsequential to how much I enjoyed this. I'll address those first, so I can gush about this novel for the rest of my review:<br><br>1) There were a few editing errors, or really more formatting issues, and at the beginning it was hard to follow, but once you realize this it's easier to keep up. I know a lot of people are put off by this (and it is slightly frustrating) but please, <i>please</i> try to get through it, you won't regret it.<br><br>3) This isn't really an annoyance as much as it is skepticism. I had a hard time believing the amount of physical activity she was capable of with Parker. I've never had cancer so I don't want to offend and say it's impossible, but I've never been in a situation where my physical pain felt nonexistent due to another person's presence. Again, I wasn't annoyed or thought it wasn't plausible, I just have never experienced it so I had a hard time relating.<br><br>3) SIGNIFICANT spoiler about the ending! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The epilogue. I didn't hate it, but it definitely gave me pause. I actually really liked getting Parker's POV and seeing how devastated he would be by her death. BUT I feel it could have been done differently. The dream felt too detailed, like maybe the author was trying too hard to get those emotions. However, there's a very good chance that I'm just bitter over how devastated I was for those 13 pages. So while I was leery of the "dream" tactic, I'll take it because I'm a HEA kind of girl and that kind of involves both people being alive. So thank God. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Now to the good stuff...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454775399ra/18013174.gif" width="450" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>-Aundrea-</b><br><br>Wow. She was unbelievably strong. I loved her meltdown in the bathroom and her internal thoughts about her situation. She recognized that being weak in a moment does not make <i>you</i> weak. She's allowed to have that moment. My God is she, after all she's been through. I would be proud to call her my friend. I honestly wish she existed and we were friends. She was so level-headed about things and recognized that even though she has cancer, it affects others, too. She was strong for herself and everyone around her. I could read every single freaking page of her life and be impressed. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458114369ra/18444347.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>-Parker-</b><br><br>I want one. Seriously. He's the very definition of a book boyfriend. I love reading about men who have their shit together, aren't afraid to go after who they want, and <i>don't</i> play games while doing so. He pursued her without pressuring her and had no problem reminding her that he was only interested in her. And all this was before he even knew about the cancer. But after? Even more freaking <i>amazing</i>. He listened to her, held her, didn't try to hide his own fears, and most importantly: didn't treat her differently. I think I loved that the most. He wasn't being extra gentle or shying away from affection for fear he would hurt her, and he was constantly forcing her out of the house when all she wanted was to hide. Love is about knowing what the person needs even if they don't, and he definitely showed that.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444611763ra/16524823.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>- Aundrea + Parker -</b><br><br>I loved the quick start and the slow build up of their relationship. I have read a lot of novels where sex is drawn out because it's the ultimate act of showing love or intimacy, and I often find myself rolling my eyes. It's almost formulaic, like we need this, this, and this and then we can have sex because it's just too big of a deal to do with someone we don't love. This is a fine opinion to have, and I'm not saying there is anything wrong with it. But not every relationship is like that, and I feel like by setting that as a standard we're saying there is something wrong about doing things any differently and that you can't possibly find your soulmate if you sleep with him/her right away. So yes, I loved the fact that they slept together on day one, where they just learned each other's names. And once they re-met, they took things slower, got to know each other, and ultimately feel in love. It was absolutely perfect in my opinion. They made each other better, and ultimately that's what a relationship should do.<br><br>The characters, the way they fit together, and the story worked so well that it isn't a surprise I was a weeping mess for half of it. I thought the author highlighted the differences in how people grieve very well. Aundrea's mom, Jean, Gemma, Jason... they all supported her differently and it was nice to read about the differences. And even though <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the cancer was on it's way to remission, Aundrea still has her heart condition to contend with. Obviously I'm not glad that she has a heart condition, but I was glad to read a novel that ended where the MC still had problems. Because meeting the love of your life doesn't take away the shiftiness of life, it just makes it a little more bearable, so I was happy to see that realistic aspect <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I would recommend this to anyone, but ready yourself with a full box of Kleenex, you WILL need it. But don't worry, it's not all sad crying, there were definitely some happy tears, too. For me, I think most of it came from the beautiful juxtaposition of such a strong woman with a disease that ultimately weakens you. The author really did an amazing job and can't wait for a continuation of Aundrea and Parker's story.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464324483ra/19226711.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Safety: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No OM drama. Minimal OW drama. There is a coworker of Parker's that is interested in him (he went on a couple dates with her prior to meeting Aundrea [but they never had sex]), and she hovers in a few scenes. But Parker is <i>very</i> clear that he isn't interested. He's really dedicated to Aundrea. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Closure: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[See spoiler #3 above. But it does end with a HEA and their story continues in book 2. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="17812968846789860637" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText16617294176483406276" style="display:none">I'll start by saying that I am a cancer survivor for 10 years now so when I read the blurb about a girl that was going through chemo and falling in love while doing it, I had to read it. Parker is super sweet and wonderful in the book. Aundrea is strong willed and determined. It was a great read that I couldn't put down even if at points it brought things a little too close to my heart and made me cry. </span>

<div id="review_790298223" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/790298223" />
    <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty"><img alt="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481371426p2/13273769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/790298223?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty">Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Farah *Professor Dean's Beauty* by: </span>
      Sara Minor
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer790298223" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7819442830683812255"><br/><br/><br/>This is such a soul touching and heartbreaking book!<br/><br/>Not your everyday kind of book, this is deep and despite the depth of the book, this is one that's going to captivate you at every single page.<br/><br/>I devoured this book in one day!<br/><br/>Aundrea McCall, is sick...<br/>Not your everyday kind of illness.<br/>She has cancer. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387223686i/7554015.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Battling the fight to survive for the last four years Aundrea is tired of it all....<br/><br/>Despite beating cancer once, it's come back. And now the treatment fierce.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387223686i/7554016.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In the darkness of her disease, she mee</span>
  <span id="freeText7819442830683812255" style="display:none"><br><br><br>This is such a soul touching and heartbreaking book!<br><br>Not your everyday kind of book, this is deep and despite the depth of the book, this is one that's going to captivate you at every single page.<br><br>I devoured this book in one day!<br><br>Aundrea McCall, is sick...<br>Not your everyday kind of illness.<br>She has cancer. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387223686i/7554015.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Battling the fight to survive for the last four years Aundrea is tired of it all....<br><br>Despite beating cancer once, it's come back. <div id="review_846273076" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/846273076" />
    <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover"><img alt="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1369044455p2/11672704.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/846273076?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover">Donna ~ The Romance Cover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer846273076" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1461731772881300404">What’s Left of Me by Amanda Maxlyn<br/>5 stars!!<br/><br/><b>“I don’t even feel like I’m a woman anymore. I look in the mirror, and all I see is this skinny, pale, empty, hairless body that has become unrecognizable. If everything that represents who I am is gone, then what’s left of me?”</b><br/><br/>This is one of those books that will stay with you for a long time! Everyone who knows me, knows that I am an emotional sap and I do cry…often, but this one had me in a complete and utter mess, I was destroyed, red puffy eyes, em</span>
  <span id="freeText1461731772881300404" style="display:none">What’s Left of Me by Amanda Maxlyn<br />5 stars!!<br /><br /><b>“I don’t even feel like I’m a woman anymore. I look in the mirror, and all I see is this skinny, pale, empty, hairless body that has become unrecognizable. If everything that represents who I am is gone, then what’s left of me?”</b><br /><br />This is one of those books that will stay with you for a long time! Everyone who knows me, knows that I am an emotional sap and I do cry…often, but this one had me in a complete and utter mess, I was destroyed, red puffy eyes, empty tear ducts, hiccups and guttural sobbing all whilst my husband slept…yes he slept through!!<br /><br />This book does tackle the “big C,” yes it is emotional, yes it is powerful, yes it is angsty, yes it is heart breaking, but it is beautifully written and takes you on one gut wrenching, awe inspiring journey. Amanda Maxlyn had me glued to this book from the first page, I could not put it down. I loved the characters, I loved the story, I loved the writing…the epilogue…is just that…the FREAKIN MOTHER OF ALL EPILOGUES…yes that is shouty caps! This book had it all, I was in the mood for a sob fest and that is exactly what I got and I devoured it…I looked awful, but hell I was willing!<br /><br />Aundrea has been dealt a crap hand of cards, she was 17 when she was first diagnosed with Hodgkin’s Lymphoma, she had beaten it once but now at the age of 21 it was time to beat it again. It was just before her course of treatment was to begin that her friends made her go out for the evening, they dressed her up and took her clubbing. She let her hair down, had a drink, had a dance and pulled…she pulled one gorgeous man called Parker…deciding to go with the flow and go against all her morals and her usual behaviour she goes back to his and has what she thinks is a one night stand…only Parker has other ideas!<br /><br /><b>“I was meant to meet Parker. He brings out the best in me. He brings out the life in me.”</b><br /><br />The trouble is with suffering with cancer, you feel like a burden, you don’t want the pity, you want to be normal and treated just like everyone else, you don’t want to have to rely on those around you for the most menial, mundane things, but sometimes, just sometimes you have to let go and take the help and the moral support you can get and this is what Aundrea finds hard. Thank god Parker has staying power, he was determined to get the girl and wanted to fight for what he thought was his, Aundrea had touched him that night and it soon became apparent that these two were meant for each other. Now we just needed Aundrea to take that leap of faith and let Parker in.<br /><br /><b>“I hate people taking care of me. I hate feeling helpless. I hate feeling lifeless…and as much as my muscles ache, and as exhausted as I am…I refuse to give in. I refuse to back down. I refuse to submit. I refuse to cry.”</b><br /><br />Aundrea though was thriving on him not knowing, she loved the fact that he treated her just like a normal person, there was no sadness, there was no pity, it was just Aundrea and Parker, Parker and Aundrea, but the trouble was, with each page you read you knew that the ball was going to get dropped and you were forever wondering what the aftermath was going to be.<br /><br />It pained me to read the lengths that Aundrea was going to, to keep the truth from Parker. It broke my heart. I just wanted her to open up and let him in. I had faith in Parker, from the get go I had a feeling that he was different, I knew that he would understand and I was willing Aundrea to just TELL HIM!! Aundrea was such a strong character though, she was tough and she was resilient and she had her “outside” face, full of bravado, but on the inside she was still this frightened girl that would cry herself to sleep at night and it pained me to read.<br /><br />This is one awe inspiring story though, through Aundrea I gained even more respect for those that suffer and beat cancer, you can never truly appreciate just what people go through, but through Aundrea’s eyes, I felt it and lived it. It is the sign of a great author if you can live and breathe a story and I did just that with this book. I was there with Aundrea every step of the way and as I said above, it hurt.<br /><br /><b>“Someone once told me that it’s not about whether there is life after you die, but whether you’re alive before you die. I didn’t believe I could ever feel alive again. Not until Parker.”</b><br /><br />Parker, what can I say, he is just the best, he was totally and utterly adorable and truly perfect for Aundrea. He was there for her when she wanted, he didn’t pity, he didn’t coddle and mother her, but he was a vital support network that she never knew she needed. I wanted to hug him hard. Everyone needs a Parker!<br /><br /><b>“You’re scared, but just because you can’t see your future, doesn’t mean I can’t. I see it clearly because I can see mine.”</b><br /><br />Amanda Maxlyn, you are a genius, this book is truly brilliant and breath taking and for a debut author I was mightily impressed. I lived and breathed this journey and for those few hours I was in another world, completely and utterly consumed in Aundrea and Parker’s story. It was a joy to read and as I said above, a story that will stay with me for a very long time. I cannot wait to see what comes next. Brilliant book, one click, you will not be disappointed.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.theromancecover.com">www.theromancecover.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="1461731772881300404" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_785557534" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/785557534" />
    <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384348451p2/5494655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/785557534?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer785557534" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3109906260604012712">This book is heavy. The harsh reality is that most of us have been affected by cancer in some way, at times I was overwhelmed. What's Left of Me is an achingly beautiful story about a young woman's struggle, not only to survive, but to overcome her fears.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>I don't even feel like a woman anymore. I look in the mirror, and all I see is this skinny, pale, empty, hairless body that has become unrecognizable. If everything that represents who I am is gone, then what's left of me.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Aundrea's life has </span>
  <span id="freeText3109906260604012712" style="display:none">This book is heavy. The harsh reality is that most of us have been affected by cancer in some way, at times I was overwhelmed. What's Left of Me is an achingly beautiful story about a young woman's struggle, not only to survive, but to overcome her fears.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I don't even feel like a woman anymore. I look in the mirror, and all I see is this skinny, pale, empty, hairless body that has become unrecognizable. If everything that represents who I am is gone, then what's left of me.</i>
</b><br /><br />Aundrea's life has revolved around her diagnosis for the past 4 years. Cancer, the hateful bitch that it is, alters all those it touches. It changes the way people see you, taking your identity. All anyone sees is the cancer. During a girls night out, Aundrea is convinced to live a little - and meets Parker (who I think may be the perfect man). Aundrea in a new city, attempts to hide behind the wig. To keep her diagnosis a secret. She isn't looking for love, but Parker is persistent. Parker makes her feel alive, and gives her something to live for. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"You're scared, but just because you can't see your future, doesn't mean that I can't. I see it clearly because I can see mine."</i>
</b><br /><br />This story has heart. An amazing debut novel. Now...the epilogue...well played Amanda. You got me. With tears steaming down my face, I may have cursed you a little bit. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3109906260604012712" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_792203143" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/792203143" />
    <a title="Johanna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10198457-johanna"><img alt="Johanna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393386564p2/10198457.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/792203143?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Johanna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Johanna" href="/user/show/10198457-johanna">Johanna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer792203143" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9185475905797606626"><b>*~*~*~3~3.5 Live life to the fullest stars*~*~*~*<br/><a href='http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/PicMonkeyCollage_zps3f427862.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387329333i/7578914._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo PicMonkeyCollage_zps3f427862.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><blockquote>Someone once told me that it's not about whether there is life after you die, but whether you're alive before you die.</blockquote></b><br/><b>
  <u>What's Left of Me</u>
</b> is a story about surviving, living, and love. We are introduced to Andrea McCall. Andrea isn't your typical 22 year old, she lives her life in fear and never foresees a future. At 17 years old she was diagnosed with cancer and went into remission. It is not until four years later that her cancer comes knocking</span>
  <span id="freeText9185475905797606626" style="display:none"><b>*~*~*~3~3.5 Live life to the fullest stars*~*~*~*<br><a href="http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/PicMonkeyCollage_zps3f427862.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387329333i/7578914._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo PicMonkeyCollage_zps3f427862.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><blockquote>Someone once told me that it's not about whether there is life after you die, but whether you're alive before you die.</blockquote></b><br><b>
  <u>What's Left of Me</u>
</b> is a story about surviving, living, and love. We are introduced to Andrea McCall. Andrea isn't your typical 22 year old, she lives her life in fear and never foresees a future. At 17 years old she was diagnosed with cancer and went into remission. It is not until four years later that her cancer comes knocking again at her doorstep. <br><a href="http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/ken-nock4_zps4d0b36bc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387508147ra/7609683.gif" alt=" photo ken-nock4_zps4d0b36bc.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>I refuse to give in.<br>I refuse to back down.<br>I refuse to submit.<br>I refuse to cry.</b><br><br>It is at this point that Andrea decides to move in with her older adopted sister, Genna, so she can receive her treatments. Andrea decides to blow off some steam and decides to have a girls night out with her best friend. While succumbing to her best friends chronic banter, Andrea decides to have a one night stand...Andddddddddd voila.. <br>Parker pops into the equation. One alcohol induced night leads to one smoking <br><a href="http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/1451516_616322471760652_44279779_n_zps46eed887.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387508147i/7609684._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1451516_616322471760652_44279779_n_zps46eed887.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>sexual encounter.<br><br>Just when Andrea thought she would never see Parker again she discovers that he works with her brother in law in a veterinary clinic.<br>Luckily for Parker, he was able to convince and forge his way into Andrea's heart but with much difficulty. As far as Andrea was concerned she didn't want a committed relationship and she definitely did not want to tell Parker about her cancer. But against all internal struggles, Andrea decides to give Parker and their non relationship a try.<br><a href="http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/quote-book-on-tumblr-take-a-chance_large_zps3dd9f963.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387508621i/7609738.jpg" alt=" photo quote-book-on-tumblr-take-a-chance_large_zps3dd9f963.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>What ends up blossoming is LOVE &lt;333<br><a href="http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/tumblr_mecjp4Cdbb1rfmf0so1_500_zpsdf5b2b80.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387508924ra/7609798.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mecjp4Cdbb1rfmf0so1_500_zpsdf5b2b80.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>I never thought of myself as one of those woman. The type who get all sappy when a man says they love them, or vice versa, but now I understand why they do, because it's in this moment that I know I've found the person I was meant to be with.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Overall, What's Left of Me was an enjoyable read. I really enjoyed Parker, and they way he became so supportive and caring. Throughout the book Parker's true intentions and feelings were displayed for Andrea to see. I never doubted his love for her... Not once...<br><br><br><b>*~*~*~*ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review*~*~*~*</b><br><br>*****Sidenote: I am honored and thrilled that I not only got to read this advanced copy but that I also personally know this wonderful, sweet, talented author. Wonderful debut novel, Amanda!!! xx</span>
  <a data-text-id="9185475905797606626" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10698753-nic?shelf=arc">arc</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer716817064" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1349759290115083659">5+++Stars WOW! What an incredible story!!! Powerful, Beautiful, Sexy! <3 <3 Make sure this one is on your TBR.<br/><br/>I have read some incredible books lately but I don't think any of them have moved me quite the way What's Left of Me by Amanda Maxlyn did! I think this is the most powerful book I have read so far in 2013 <3 I remember reading the prologue thinking, this books is going to completely destroy me and I'm happy to report it did not! Now that being said, I was taken on one hell of an incredib</span>
  <span id="freeText1349759290115083659" style="display:none">5+++Stars WOW! What an incredible story!!! Powerful, Beautiful, Sexy! &lt;3 &lt;3 Make sure this one is on your TBR.<br /><br />I have read some incredible books lately but I don't think any of them have moved me quite the way What's Left of Me by Amanda Maxlyn did! I think this is the most powerful book I have read so far in 2013 &lt;3 I remember reading the prologue thinking, this books is going to completely destroy me and I'm happy to report it did not! Now that being said, I was taken on one hell of an incredible emotional journey.<br /><br />It's hard to read this story without wondering if Aundrea is a real person. Everything this character experiences felt so real I couldn't imagine that she was a creation of someone's imagination. Seriously, one of the most amazing characters I have ever read. I loved every character in this story, Parker is swoon worthy and perfect and I was on edge wondering what would happen next with him. Then there was Genna. I love this amazing character so deeply, the story wouldn't have been the same without her. Amanda Maxlyn, you blow my mind with your character development.<br /><br />What's left of me will captivate you within the first few pages and keep you wanting more. It's brilliant characters will steal your heart and the storyline will have you on the edge of your seat. Emotional and raw, you will be in awe of Aundrea and her journey. Not only is What's Left of Me powerful and emotional, it's sexy as hell! Way to write sexiness Amanda Maxlyn, you rocked it! Just the right amount of hot sexiness to make my heart melt and my pulse soar!<br /><br />I could envision What's Left of Me being made into a movie as one played out in my head while I turned each page! I can't stress enough how incredible this book was. If you love heartfelt emotional books but want a little sexiness too, What's Left Of Me should be your next read.<br /><br />Release Date: December 13th</span>

<div id="review_833966553" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/833966553" />
    <a title="Amanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13536962-amanda"><img alt="Amanda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499591290p2/13536962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/833966553?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda" href="/user/show/13536962-amanda">Amanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13536962-amanda?shelf=04-new-adult">04-new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13536962-amanda?shelf=05-romance">05-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13536962-amanda?shelf=00-2015">00-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13536962-amanda?shelf=16-authors-to-read">16-authors-to-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13536962-amanda?shelf=01-2010s">01-2010s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13536962-amanda?shelf=14-new-adult-project">14-new-adult-project</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13536962-amanda?shelf=04-contemporary">04-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer833966553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9001610453351308769"><a href='http://s1272.photobucket.com/user/ameh2/media/da3b031d345be1fa23a11bdd86be7717_zps5qkubftf.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425637231i/13913363.png' alt=' photo da3b031d345be1fa23a11bdd86be7717_zps5qkubftf.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>Items ticked off: 10</b><br/><br/>Despite what my status updates on this book might imply, I did like this one. When it comes to NA, I rarely say that. For a New Adult story this is a really good one. It never felt too tropey, and that's one gigant plus in my book these days. A New Adult story that isn't tropey, believe that I will be all over it. And I was. <i>What's Left of Me</i> is much enjoyed by my friends and I had high expectations, maybe a little too high. <br/><br/><i>What's Left of Me</i> is the story of Aundrea. She'</span>
  <span id="freeText9001610453351308769" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1272.photobucket.com/user/ameh2/media/da3b031d345be1fa23a11bdd86be7717_zps5qkubftf.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425637231i/13913363.png" alt=" photo da3b031d345be1fa23a11bdd86be7717_zps5qkubftf.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>Items ticked off: 10</b><br><br>Despite what my status updates on this book might imply, I did like this one. When it comes to NA, I rarely say that. For a New Adult story this is a really good one. It never felt too tropey, and that's one gigant plus in my book these days. A New Adult story that isn't tropey, believe that I will be all over it. And I was. <i>What's Left of Me</i> is much enjoyed by my friends and I had high expectations, maybe a little too high. <br><br><i>What's Left of Me</i> is the story of Aundrea. She's been fighting cancer for the better part of her life and is getting tired of the way the illness dictates her life. Her character is easy to feel for, and unlike some NA heroines, I was rooting for her all the way through. Despite her luck, or lack thereof, she tries to make the best out of it. Sure, she has her issues and that's understandable. All in all, she's a great character. Truly, she and all the other characters were lovable with all their ups and downs. Heck, this might be the best set of characters in a NA story I've read in quite some time. <br><br>The thing though, bringing this story down to a three star rating is the romance. <i>I know, I sound cold-hearted. Promise, I'm not</i>. As said, I liked the characters so I should be loving the romance. However, insta love isn't for me, and that's what we get (more or less). It's hard to feel chemistry between characters when it's put into words rather than shown. <b>I need a little substance to my romance</b>. The hero fell too fast for me to understand his infatuation with Aundrea in the first place. So I never fell for them as a couple, and since the story focused mostly on the relationship and Aundrea's reactions to it more than it focused on her struggling with her illness, the story lost some of the deeper emotional substance.<br><br>I want to make it clear that despite my issues, <i>What's Left of Me</i> is much better than the average NA story. It offers more than trivial issues and isn't littered with stereotypes and constant slut-shaming. The characters are well developed, the general story has substance, and the writing is decent. I believe people will like this more than I did since it's mainly personal issues I had with this one and other people will react different to the romance (perhaps enjoy it more than I did). All in all, a great NA story, and I don't say that lightly. <br><br>| <a href="http://amandasays.booklikes.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">BookLikes</a> | <a href="https://www.leafmarks.com/AmandaSays" rel="nofollow noopener">Leafmarks</a> |</span>
  <a data-text-id="9001610453351308769" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_786199875" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/786199875" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/786199875?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer786199875" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6552301354411312029"><b>When stars really don't matter…until they do, but then they don't…or do they?</b><br/><br/>WHY AM I ALWAYS THE ONLY ONE!!<br/><br/>Okay so maybe I'm not the only one, but I seem to be one of the first people not shitting tears or wanting to make sweet sweet love to this book. Maybe my heart is defective, or maybe just maybe…I have a good reason for my rating. I'll attempt to explain.<br/><br/>Amanda Maxlyn <i>can</i> write! How many times have I reviewed a book where I incessantly complain about how I liked the "idea" of a book or love</span>
  <span id="freeText6552301354411312029" style="display:none"><b>When stars really don't matter…until they do, but then they don't…or do they?</b><br /><br />WHY AM I ALWAYS THE ONLY ONE!!<br /><br />Okay so maybe I'm not the only one, but I seem to be one of the first people not shitting tears or wanting to make sweet sweet love to this book. Maybe my heart is defective, or maybe just maybe…I have a good reason for my rating. I'll attempt to explain.<br /><br />Amanda Maxlyn <i>can</i> write! How many times have I reviewed a book where I incessantly complain about how I liked the "idea" of a book or loved the "concept". Countless reviews explaining that it wasn't about the story the author was trying to tell, but the execution….the writing. Being an author is more than having an amazing idea, a beautiful story in your head. Those ideas have to translate onto paper. An author has to write. You, Amanda Maxlyn, can write. <br /><br /><i>What's Left of Me</i> is a beautiful story, a good story, but it lacked to give me something that elicited an emotional response. The story wasn't anything I hadn't read before. I could tell where the story was going before it went there, and it was so reminiscent of other books I've read with similar plots. The author definitely made the characters her own, and wrote beautifully, but I needed more from the plot. What can I say; I'm greedy like that. <br /><br />Now onto what made my final thought of this book be, "son of a bitch"...the epilogue. The epilogue made me want to slap Amanda Maxlyn's ass in a job well done! <i>That</i> is the type of writing and emotional solicitation that creates amazing books. If the author could have done that with my emotions the entire book, my rating would have been five stars easy.<br /><br />However, in the end, the beautiful writing and beautiful moments just weren't enough for me to overlook the feeling that there was something missing. <br /><br />So yes, this was a good book, but saying it was great solely based off the epilogue heard round the world just wouldn't be fair. I needed more from the story.<br /><br />Either way, I am very excited and intrigued to see what Ms. Maxlyn has in store for us next.<br /><br />READ ON!</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_794560683" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/794560683" />
    <a title="Beth " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6473076-beth"><img alt="Beth " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1490276204p2/6473076.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/794560683?book_show_action=true">Dec 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth " href="/user/show/6473076-beth">Beth </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer794560683" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12316681076290351261">Amanda Maxlyn is a debut author? This is her first published book? I can't freakin' believe it because she knocked it out of the park with WHAT'S LEFT OF ME. I have read so many great books lately from some established authors and Amanda is right there with the best of them. Frankly, WHAT'S LEFT OF ME is as honest and emotionally gripping as anything you would read from Colleen Hoover.<br/><br/>This book hooked me right out of the gate. The first ten percent was smoking' H-O-T! I was literally fanning mys</span>
  <span id="freeText12316681076290351261" style="display:none">Amanda Maxlyn is a debut author? This is her first published book? I can't freakin' believe it because she knocked it out of the park with WHAT'S LEFT OF ME. I have read so many great books lately from some established authors and Amanda is right there with the best of them. Frankly, WHAT'S LEFT OF ME is as honest and emotionally gripping as anything you would read from Colleen Hoover.<br /><br />This book hooked me right out of the gate. The first ten percent was smoking' H-O-T! I was literally fanning myself after that sizzling start. But, don't think this book is all about sex because it is so much more than that. The plot and character development is exceptional. There was no part of this book where I was bored or unhappy with the way the story was going. The story line was very smooth.<br /><br />I must warn you, WHAT'S LEFT OF ME is also an emotional tear-jerker. I went through several tissues over the course of reading. The personal and physical struggles Aundrea endures over the course of the book broke me down into a blubbering mess. I felt I was right there by her side the entire time experiencing every shattering development of her life. <br /><br />Aundrea's rock and most definitely her Prince Charming is Parker. What a wonderful man he is! He came into her life at exactly the right time. Right when she needed him most. Their first meeting is not how you would expect two lovers two meet and have a lasting relationship. Even when Aundrea thinks she is losing her battle, herself Parker never lets her give up. He is her strength through pain, her distraction when the pain is unbearable. <br /><br />By the end of this book I was crying, shocked, and speechless. I cannot wait to read more from the author and hopefully, more about these characters. A round of applause for Amanda Maxlyn!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12316681076290351261" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_803168980" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/803168980" />
    <a title="Katie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3796016-katie"><img alt="Katie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1295562881p2/3796016.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/803168980?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie" href="/user/show/3796016-katie">Katie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer803168980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16655394037874263066">I wonder what other people think of this heroine... The struggles she's had, the way she pushes the hero away. Her worries about things that may seem insignificant to those who've never experienced what she has and continues to experience time and time again. <br/><br/>I personally judge this subject matter very harshly. Having gone through (very similar) cancer treatments in my 20s as Aundrea, it is very important to me as a reader that the author does the homework and get the emotions pertaining to the </span>
  <span id="freeText16655394037874263066" style="display:none">I wonder what other people think of this heroine... The struggles she's had, the way she pushes the hero away. Her worries about things that may seem insignificant to those who've never experienced what she has and continues to experience time and time again. <br /><br />I personally judge this subject matter very harshly. Having gone through (very similar) cancer treatments in my 20s as Aundrea, it is very important to me as a reader that the author does the homework and get the emotions pertaining to the illness (and most especially the treatments) right. I have never read anything in which the author got the emotional aspects of a cancer victim's struggles with treatments so accurate. In many cases it isn't the cancer itself that causes the sickness, it's the damn aggressive treatments. There were times I felt as if Aundrea's thoughts and feelings were pulled from my own head 10 years ago. Everything that Aundrea struggled with... I had tears in my eyes throughout this entire book. Having to wear an itchy wig. The zolfran for the nausea. The fatigue, which I always thought was the worst! Which then meant Nuelasta shots. The mediport. The pokes and prods from needles that after so many times just doesn't matter anymore. Even the descriptions of when someone goes to a chemotherapy treatment. Sitting there for literally hours and watching actual poison being pumped into your body. Knowing that by the next day you're going to feel like you're actually dying. These descriptions gave me the chills! And finally, most especially when you've lost not only the hair on the top of your head but your eyebrows and eyelashes. At that point there is no hiding it anymore. When you feel like you don't know and can't trust your own body because of all the crazy side effects that they can't predict you'll have... You become a stranger inside of your own skin. <br /><br />As crazy as it is, this book paralleled my own life almost eerily. My now husband and I began dating during my first chemo treatments. The fears that Aundrea had about her wig falling off... All though my husband and I had been friends prior to dating, and he knew I was going through treatments, I never let him see me without my wig on. I was so afraid that if he saw me without hair it would scare him off. I now know that nothing pertaining to my sickness ever would have. There were many situations when I could understand that a reader may have become annoyed with Audrea and how she continuously kept shoving Parker away. But when your not comfortable with yourself, how can you trust that someone else, especially a virtual stranger will look past something so scary? I knew why she did it and I loved her all the more for it. I even remember having to schedule the time I would spend with my husband in those first months around my treatments. They were every two weeks which meant the week after chemo I could never let him see me. That following week, when it was almost back to normal... was when we would hang out. <br /><br />There were several other very specific descriptions that I could relate to but this review is supposed to be about What's Left of Me, not "me"... I guess what I'm mostly trying to convey is this book was outstanding. It's raw, it's real and I couldn't have loved it more. With all the stories coming out now with book two being from "his" point of view, I can only wish Amanda Maxlyn provides us with Parker's side of the story. I know how Aundrea dealt with her struggle, I want to know how Parker dealt with it. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16655394037874263066" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
