<div id="review_791920205" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/791920205" />
    <a title="Three Chicks" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20696685-three-chicks"><img alt="Three Chicks" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1369511277p2/20696685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/791920205?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Three Chicks" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Three Chicks" href="/user/show/20696685-three-chicks">Three Chicks</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer791920205" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer316657906693006633"><br/>Aundrea (her friends call her Dre) has been battling Hodgkin's Lymphoma since she was 17. She is at the point in her disease that her treatment is no longer effective and a bone marrow transplant (from her own marrow) is necessary. She has some strong chemo treatments that she needs to get through so she can receive the transplant. She is staying with her sister and her brother-in-law. Her parents have made numerous financial sacrifices for her-they lost their house in the process of paying her </span>
  <span id="freeText316657906693006633" style="display:none"><br />Aundrea (her friends call her Dre) has been battling Hodgkin's Lymphoma since she was 17. She is at the point in her disease that her treatment is no longer effective and a bone marrow transplant (from her own marrow) is necessary. She has some strong chemo treatments that she needs to get through so she can receive the transplant. She is staying with her sister and her brother-in-law. Her parents have made numerous financial sacrifices for her-they lost their house in the process of paying her medical bills and Dre has guilt on top of guilt for being the one that was the catalyst for that.<br /><br />She is taking a few on- line courses in college. She had to be home schooled towards the end of high school because of her treatments, and so she missed her prom, and graduation and parties and her senior week trip. Her boyfriend (the only one she ever had and her lone sexual partner) broke things off after she was diagnosed. She doesn't blame him-not many guys would stick around and put themselves through her turmoil.<br /><br /><br />She has a strong support system in her friends. They want her to loosen up, to enjoy her life as best she can. They drag her to a club and insist she dress for party mode. She loosens up to the point that she engages in flirting with the gorgeous guy who she finds is eyeball fu*#ing her. The two of them are doing their own version of Dirty Dancing and they carry it out of the club. She goes home with him and has her first one night stand. Let's just say a good time was had by all! She sneaks out the next day. She knows this can't go anywhere, whether she wants it to or not.<br /><br /><br />Her brother-in-law is a veterinarian and owns his own practice. The next day he invites his new partner to dinner and it's a case of guess who's coming to dinner. She sees Parker and he is even more gorgeous than she first thought. He tries to get her alone to talk about what happened the night before but she puts the kibosh on that and tells him it was a one time thing.<br /><br /><b>Look, Parker, I don't usually go home with strange men, or strangers for that matter. I promise after this moment I won't bring up last night again, or even think about it. It won't happen again, and I swear I won't tell Jason. So, your secret of screwing the boss' sister-in-law is safe with me.</b><br /><br /><b>You think I'm strange?</b><br /><br />He lets her know that may be her intention for things to end, but it's not his!<br /><br />Dre agrees to help out her brother- in- law a few times a week. And yeah, maybe she wouldn't mind seeing Parker there. This guy is the whole package-he's smart, compassionate, witty is soft on the eyes and makes no bones about the fact that he wants Dre-big time wants her in his life!<br /><br />They hang out a little together and it's apparent they both have feelings for one another. Dre won't tell him that she has cancer. She isn't ready to lose him yet-everyone knows no one wants the girl with cancer. She doesn't want to see that look in his eyes that people get when they find out she is sick. <br /><br /><b>I'm not ready for him to go running. Maybe I'm being selfish. I am selfish. I want to keep him around, but I don't want to share anything personal. Is that too much to ask?</b><br /><br />Meanwhile, she is suffering through this latest course of chemo, she is sick and weak and depressed. She comes up with excuses for her absences from Parker's life. <br /><br /><br />This is told for the most part in her POV. Every description of her treatment, her pain, her nausea her devastating loss of hair, resonates with the reader. I became this girl I was so immersed in her life, when she allowed herself to cry I cried right along with her. I cried for her when she woudn't allow herself to cry, but I wished she would. And through the tears, she always tempered it with laughter, with her unique way of saying that if someone had to bear this burden, better her than someone she loved. <br /><br /><b>There is nothing worse than taking a shower and pulling out clumps of hair or watching them stick to your wet body.</b><br /><br /><b>I make my way to the mirror and stare at the unrecognizable person in the mirror. My lips look more chapped than I remember. My ears point out further than I thought, my eyebrows look misplaced and my eyes suddenly seem to sit much further apart. I don't recognize the woman looking back at me. She's not me. She's a stranger.</b><br /><br />So much of her emotions evolved around Parker and her need to cover up her secret. Even the wigs she wears are a burden, she fears every time he runs his hands through her hair he will dislodge one. <br /><br /><b>I can feel the wetness along with pressure between my thighs build and no matter what, I don't want to stop. I don't think I can stop. Until I feel his hand move into my hair. He grips my wig, tugging slightly, causing my eyes to pop open. "Parker! Wait!" I shriek.</b><br /><br />One of my favorite things about Dre is her passion for reading. Her Kindle goes everywhere with her. <br /><br /><b>I can't pick a favorite book, explaining that it's not about what or who is the best, but rather the story itself. Each book is different and unique, bringing out the best emotions in me. I love getting pulled out of reality-away from the reminders of my pain.</b><br /><br />There are complications upon complications thrown in this girl's face. And always there is the secret-what will happen when Parker learns the truth? What will happen to Dre if the transplant fails?<br /><br /><b>We all have an end date. We know we're going to die. The only question is when. It's the not knowing-or the someday-that makes it easy to not think about.</b> <br /><br /><br />I adored this book! I thought it would be sad and depressing, and although at times it was those things, it was funny and hot and light. Parker may not be an MMA fighter, or a rock star or a billionaire. He may just be a man who treats animals for a living. But this guy-he is the stuff heroes are made of-true and honest and real. This guy, he stole my heart. He's the one that every girl should dream about, should long for, should share a first kiss. <br /><br /><br />The question everyone wants answered-does Dre die? I will only say that you will need tissues, plenty of tissues. One for the happy tears that will surely flow and ones for the tears that will break your heart. <br /><br /><b>"I know that no matter how hard life gets, it's amazing to just be here. To be alive."</b><br /><br /><b>"We'll take it day by day. Together. I just got you and I refuse to let you go."</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="316657906693006633" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_752317273" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/752317273" />
    <a title="Sue" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7377874-sue"><img alt="Sue" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594207220p2/7377874.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/752317273?book_show_action=true">Oct 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sue" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sue" href="/user/show/7377874-sue">Sue</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer752317273" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16034068559187264871">I was gifted this book to read by the author Amanda Maxlyn. I had the pleasure of reading this as an ARC and let me say, it was a delight to read.<br/><br/>A young girl going through the throws of Cancer, finding herself undergoing yet more treatment, having to wear a wig that was not obvious to people who had not met her before.<br/>All she wanted, was to be treated 'normal'. Not for people to see her and the cancer. Just her.<br/><br/>She goes out one night with friends in the haste to be accepted and just be a normal</span>
  <span id="freeText16034068559187264871" style="display:none">I was gifted this book to read by the author Amanda Maxlyn. I had the pleasure of reading this as an ARC and let me say, it was a delight to read.<br /><br />A young girl going through the throws of Cancer, finding herself undergoing yet more treatment, having to wear a wig that was not obvious to people who had not met her before.<br />All she wanted, was to be treated 'normal'. Not for people to see her and the cancer. Just her.<br /><br />She goes out one night with friends in the haste to be accepted and just be a normal young woman about town when she comes upon a lovely guy. She has a bit too much to drink, but things did stop before she took it things further with him. It was 'just' a night out, right?<br /><br />Onwards in the book you see her struggle with telling the only person who has ever got close to her in a while about the fact, she's ill. She's been struggling to get her identity back, to get the girl back she once was, to get people to see HER for herself and definitely not to feel sorry for her. <br /><br />The tale is poignant. We have either faced the big C word ourselves or have known people or know people now who are experiencing this illness. <br /><br />I thought the author wrote a brilliant story, and seeing its the only book I have ever read by her I won't pass on reading any further books she may throw my way.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16034068559187264871" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4053726366618964128"><br/>Life works in mysterious ways.<br/><br/>Four years ago I became known as the girl with cancer.<br/><br/>I refuse to cry.<br/><br/>And I refuse to give in.<br/><br/>A relationship with a man is the last thing I’m looking for right now, but one night with Parker changes everything. He is persistent, and he knows what he wants. Me.<br/><br/>He doesn’t treat me like I’m fragile.<br/><br/>But he doesn’t know, and I’m not ready to tell him.<br/><br/>What if it changes everything?<br/><br/>Tragedy found me when I was seventeen.<br/><br/>Love found me when I was twenty-one.<br/><br/>My name is Aundrea</span>
  <span id="freeText4053726366618964128" style="display:none"><br>Life works in mysterious ways.<br><br>Four years ago I became known as the girl with cancer.<br><br>I refuse to cry.<br><br>And I refuse to give in.<br><br>A relationship with a man is the last thing I’m looking for right now, but one night with Parker changes everything. He is persistent, and he knows what he wants. Me.<br><br>He doesn’t treat me like I’m fragile.<br><br>But he doesn’t know, and I’m not ready to tell him.<br><br>What if it changes everything?<br><br>Tragedy found me when I was seventeen.<br><br>Love found me when I was twenty-one.<br><br>My name is Aundrea McCall, and this is my journey.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411937235i/11302508._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><br>Holy cow!<br>Be prepared for some ugly crying, actually for a lot of ugly crying.<br>This book is so hearth-breakingly beautiful, I just can't put it into words.<br><br>I felt as though Andrea was one of my closest friends and everything she was going through effected me. I cried through all the chemo treatments with her, through every tear she shed I was right there with her.<br><br>The epilogue? Jeez, my eyes are still puffy!!! That was a mean mean trick :(<br><br>It was beautiful, it was heartfelt an emotional rollercoaster, but I'm so glad I went on this journey with her.<br>Now all I need is live Parker and I will be good to go.<br></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411937235i/11302509._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <a title="VEL" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14418871-vel"><img alt="VEL" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420839307p2/14418871.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/846397457?book_show_action=true">Feb 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="VEL" class="user" itemprop="url" name="VEL" href="/user/show/14418871-vel">VEL</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer846397457" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13693468544828280236">You know from the synopsis that this is likely to be an emotional book!<br/><br/>Amanda Maxlyn sure does get your emotions rolling! <br/><br/>Aundrea is a strong, level headed, beautiful lady suffering from Cancer. The author really draws you with how she is dealing with this disease, in fact you feel as if you are physically with her holding her hand! <br/><br/>Then we have the charismatic, absolutely adorable Parker. They have good chemistry between them. A one night stand is what she needs, to be young carefree and for on</span>
  <span id="freeText13693468544828280236" style="display:none">You know from the synopsis that this is likely to be an emotional book!<br /><br />Amanda Maxlyn sure does get your emotions rolling! <br /><br />Aundrea is a strong, level headed, beautiful lady suffering from Cancer. The author really draws you with how she is dealing with this disease, in fact you feel as if you are physically with her holding her hand! <br /><br />Then we have the charismatic, absolutely adorable Parker. They have good chemistry between them. A one night stand is what she needs, to be young carefree and for once just be like every other girl, party and have fun.<br /><br />But how long will she be able to hide her secret. Will Parker stay by her side? Or will he just not be able to handle &amp; want nothing to do with her? <br /><br />Well to find out the answers you are going to have to read this book, it's great. Beautifully written, drawing you in and seeing another side to someone who has a disease that you have no answers to or what your future will hold. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13693468544828280236" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('70xamk7wghCf55Abu6y40MYiUcZLhPwZWOo5v8T9WmdIjCJ2bmrjdYK6+SOq7I9HREl0E68CbunkFB386Ig0wg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2it0+pOT9/Z2XSCLF6R1uEbnC13IjEcH09N3ThxuywR96wwWswmWk2sASbMG5EIvxIwuiCwK1fdvLVMNMBuloQ==')})
  }

It means I have something to do, or somewhere else to be, other than at home, sick and feeling helpless.&rdquo;</span>

        first.parentNode.insertBefore(script, first);
      }
    }
  if (w.attachEvent) {
    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
  }
}(window, document,
    ['//assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js',
     '//apis.google.com/js/plusone.js'
    ]
  ));

//]]>
</script>

      </div>

    </div>
